## Affiliate Marketing

| [Parabola](https://parabola.io) | Drag-and-drop productivity tool for automating data workflows [(pricing)](https://parabola.io/pricing)/[(quick start)](https://parabola.io/getting-started) | Limited free plan with core features | <br>• Visual flow builder<br>• Data transformation<br>• Integrations with popular tools<br>• Scheduled runs | <br>• Powerful data manipulation capabilities<br>• No coding required for most tasks<br>• Good for marketing and e-commerce automation | <br>• Learning curve for complex data operations<br>• Primarily focused on data workflows | 4/5 | 3/5 | 3/5 | Create and sell Parabola flow templates, offer data automation consulting |
| [Phantombuster](https://phantombuster.com) | Automation and data extraction platform for sales and marketing [(pricing)](https://phantombuster.com/pricing)/[(quick start)](https://phantombuster.com/blog/guides/how-to-use-phantombuster-2HPZ2) | 14-day free trial | <br>• Ready-made automation scripts<br>• Data extraction<br>• API integrations<br>• Cloud-based execution | <br>• Specialized for sales and marketing<br>• Large library of pre-built automations<br>• No coding required for basic use | <br>• Focused on specific use cases<br>• Can be expensive for high-volume usage | 4/5 | 3/5 | 3/5 | Create and sell custom Phantoms (automation scripts), offer data services |
| [Automa](https://www.automa.tech) | Browser extension for automating web-based tasks [(pricing)](https://www.automa.tech)/[(quick start)](https://docs.automa.tech) | Free for personal use with some limitations | <br>• Visual workflow builder<br>• Web scraping<br>• Form filling<br>• Browser automation | <br>• Easy to use for browser-based tasks<br>• No coding required for basic automations<br>• Works across different websites | <br>• Limited to browser-based automations<br>• May require premium for advanced features | 4/5 | 3/5 | 3/5 | Develop and sell Automa workflow templates, offer web automation consulting |
| [NocoDB](https://www.nocodb.com) | An open-source Airtable alternative that turns any database into a smart spreadsheet with automation capabilities. [(pricing)](https://www.nocodb.com/pricing)/[(quick start)](https://docs.nocodb.com/getting-started) | Free and open-source, self-hosted or cloud options available | <br>• Database to spreadsheet interface<br>• Multiple view types<br>• Automations and webhooks<br>• Role-based access control | <br>• Open-source and customizable<br>• Familiar spreadsheet-like interface<br>• Can work with existing databases | <br>• Requires some technical knowledge for setup<br>• Fewer integrations compared to Airtable | 4/5 | 3/5 | 3/5 | Offer NocoDB setup and customization services, develop and sell plugins or extensions |

## Online Education & Courses
